        let activeFilter = 'All';
        let chartInstance = null;

        function formatCurrency(val) {
            return Number(val).toLocaleString('pt-BR', {minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2});
        }

        function getStatusClass(status) {
            if(status.includes('Approved')) return 'status-Approved';
            if(status.includes('Failed')) return 'status-Failed';
            if(status.includes('CANCELED')) return 'status-CANCELED';
            if(status.includes('progress')) return 'status-In-progress';
            return 'status-Unknown';
        }

        function setFilter(status) {
            activeFilter = status;
            
            document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.remove('active');
                if (btn.classList.contains(status.split(' ')[0]) || 
                   (status === 'All' && btn.classList.contains('All'))) {
                    btn.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
            
            applyFilters();
        }

        function applyFilters() {
            const query = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
            
            let filteredData = rawData.filter(row => {
                const desc = (row['Item description'] || '').toLowerCase();
                const comp = (row['Winning company'] || '').toLowerCase();
                const notice = (row['Notice'] || '').toLowerCase();
                const matchSearch = desc.includes(query) || comp.includes(query) || notice.includes(query);
                
                const matchStatus = activeFilter === 'All' || row['Eletronic Bidding status'].includes(activeFilter);
                
                return matchSearch && matchStatus;
            });

            // Sorting Logic
            const sortVal = document.getElementById('sortSelect').value;
            if (sortVal === 'az-desc') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => (a['Item description'] || '').localeCompare(b['Item description'] || ''));
            } else if (sortVal === 'za-desc') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => (b['Item description'] || '').localeCompare(a['Item description'] || ''));
            } else if (sortVal === 'min-est') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => a['Estimated Total Value BID'] - b['Estimated Total Value BID']);
            } else if (sortVal === 'max-est') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => b['Estimated Total Value BID'] - a['Estimated Total Value BID']);
            } else if (sortVal === 'min-neg') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => a['Total value'] - b['Total value']);
            } else if (sortVal === 'max-neg') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => b['Total value'] - a['Total value']);
            } else if (sortVal === 'max-unit-est') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => b['Estimated unity value BID'] - a['Estimated unity value BID']);
            } else if (sortVal === 'max-unit-neg') {
                filteredData.sort((a, b) => b['Unit value'] - a['Unit value']);
            }

            updateKPIs(filteredData);
            renderTable(filteredData);
            updateChart(filteredData);
        }

        function updateKPIs(data) {
            const count = data.length;
            const totalEst = data.reduce((sum, row) => sum + (row['Estimated Total Value BID'] || 0), 0);
            const totalNeg = data.reduce((sum, row) => sum + (row['Total value'] || 0), 0);
            const sumUnitEst = data.reduce((sum, row) => sum + (row['Estimated unity value BID'] || 0), 0);
            const sumUnitNeg = data.reduce((sum, row) => sum + (row['Unit value'] || 0), 0);

            document.getElementById('kpiCount').textContent = count;
            document.getElementById('kpiEst').textContent = 'R$ ' + formatCurrency(totalEst);
            document.getElementById('kpiNeg').textContent = 'R$ ' + formatCurrency(totalNeg);
            
            // Avoid division by zero
            document.getElementById('kpiUnitEst').textContent = count > 0 ? 'R$ ' + formatCurrency(sumUnitEst / count) : 'R$ 0,00';
            document.getElementById('kpiUnitNeg').textContent = count > 0 ? 'R$ ' + formatCurrency(sumUnitNeg / count) : 'R$ 0,00';
        }

        function renderTable(dataset) {
            const tbody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
            tbody.innerHTML = '';
            
            // NO LIMITATION! Showing all items requested.
            const displayData = dataset; 

            displayData.forEach(row => {
                let desc = row['Item description'] || '';
                if(desc.length > 50) desc = desc.substring(0, 50) + '...';
                
                const tr = document.createElement('tr');
                tr.innerHTML = `
                    <td>${row['Notice']}</td>
                    <td title="${row['Item description']}">${desc}</td>
                    <td>${row['Winning company']}</td>
                    <td>R$ ${formatCurrency(row['Estimated unity value BID'])}</td>
                    <td>R$ ${formatCurrency(row['Unit value'])}</td>
                    <td>R$ ${formatCurrency(row['Estimated Total Value BID'])}</td>
                    <td>R$ ${formatCurrency(row['Total value'])}</td>
                    <td><span class="status-badge ${getStatusClass(row['Eletronic Bidding status'])}">${row['Eletronic Bidding status']}</span></td>
                `;
                tbody.appendChild(tr);
            });
        }

        function updateChart(data) {
            const ctx = document.getElementById('statusChart').getContext('2d');
            
            let countApp = 0, countFail = 0, countCanc = 0, countProg = 0;

            data.forEach(row => {
                const s = row['Eletronic Bidding status'];
                if(s.includes('Approved')) countApp++;
                else if(s.includes('Failed')) countFail++;
                else if(s.includes('CANCELED')) countCanc++;
                else if(s.includes('progress')) countProg++;
            });

            if (chartInstance) {
                chartInstance.destroy();
            }

            chartInstance = new Chart(ctx, {
                type: 'doughnut',
                data: {
                    labels: ['Aprovados', 'Fracassados', 'Cancelados', 'Em Progresso'],
                    datasets: [{
                        data: [countApp, countFail, countCanc, countProg],
                        backgroundColor: ['#11734b', '#b10202', '#3d3d3d', '#eb5d0b']
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: { position: 'bottom' }
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        window.onload = () => applyFilters();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
